On the other hand, it can play almost every Media Video or Audio Format that exists (over 200 media formats are supported!). \r\n_____________________________________________________________\r\nIn addition, The DVD Player+ supports some unique Features that you will not find on any other Player: \r\n- When you insert a DVD disc with a movie, it automatically find and display all available Movie Information for the movie (actors, plot, authors, the original Film Poster, etc)\r\n- Also, you will get direct access to the any official extra videos and clips for the movie \r\n- Automatically load all Media (Video/Audio) Disc contents during swap of DVD’s\r\n- The Video Player brings to you 14 High-Quality, custom-made Visual Effects for the Video.\r\n- A real-time 2D to 3D conversion during playback, so the 2D Video is viewed as a 3D one (with anaglyph glasses)\r\n- Adjust the brightness, the saturation and the contrast of the video (for dark videos) \r\n- Rotate the video with 6 options (vertically, flip horizontally, etc) \r\n- Capture snapshots from the video and auto-save them to the Pictures folder during playback \r\n- Replay, Play, Pause, Move back or forward, Skip positions \r\n- Full Screen View or Normal View \r\n- Adjust the volume \r\n- Switch modes without stop \r\n\r\nVIDEO EFFECTS \r\n_________________________________ \r\nYou can play every video in your PC in 14 different modes: \r\n- 2D: classic mode, \r\n- 3D: watch your 2D recorded video in 3D (watch with anaglyph glasses \r\n– 6 types of glasses supported) \r\n- Cartoon mode: watch yourself in a cartoon mode!
